[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the Mongoose HTTP [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary during fuzzing tests. The overflow occurs when writing [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte beyond the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds of a stack-allocated variable `tmp371` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes, located at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the `mg_vxprintf` function. The write occurs at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m, which is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after the end of this buffer. AddressSanitizer has assigned this issue [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma scariness score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m, categorizing it as a [0m[32m"1-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow."[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is a **stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability** that manifests during the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution of formatted output operations within the Mongoose library's printf [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation. Specifically, the vulnerability involves a single-byte write [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation that exceeds the bounds of a stack-allocated buffer.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location of Overflow**: The overflow occurs in the `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction called from `mg_putchar_iobuf_static`, which is part of the string copying[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`scpy`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m within `mg_vxprintf`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Chain**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following execution [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_http_parse` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHTTP parsing entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_log` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlogging function[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_vxprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mformatted printing[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_snprintf` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `mg_vsnprintf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstring formatting[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_dtoa` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble-to-ASCII conversion[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Back to `mg_vxprintf`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `scpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstring copy[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_putchar_iobuf_static`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhere the overflow occurs[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Affected Buffer**: The stack frame analysis reveals:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The frame contains two objects: `tmp` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m72[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tmp371` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The memory access occurs at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m, which is exactly at the boundary after[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tmp371`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This represents a single-byte overflow past the end of the buffer[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Context**: The vulnerability is triggered during HTTP parsing operations, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically when logging functionality is invoked, which subsequently calls [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting functions that perform double-to-ASCII conversions.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msections should be examined:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **src/printf.c**: The `mg_pfn_iobuf_private` and `mg_putchar_iobuf_static` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions where the actual overflow write occurs[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **src/fmt.c**: [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `mg_vxprintf` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m247[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m323[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m where the vulnerable buffers are [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `scpy` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m233[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that performs the string copying[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `mg_dtoa` function that handles double-to-ASCII conversion[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **src/log.c**: The `mg_log` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m43[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand how logging [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggers the vulnerable code path[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **src/http.c**: The `mg_http_parse` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m317[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry point that leads to the vulnerability[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Buffer Size Calculations**: The code sections responsible for determining [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer sizes, particularly for the [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte `tmp371` variable and how it interacts [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the writing operations[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to be related to insufficient buffer size allocation or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minadequate bounds checking during formatted output operations, particularly in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenarios involving floating-point number formatting within the logging subsystem [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered by HTTP parsing operations.[0m                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m327[0m[39m:          n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmongoose.[0m[1;92mc:819[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m829[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m819[0m[39m:      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'E'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m820[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m  char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m821[0m[39m:          double d = [0m[1;35mva_arg[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*ap, double[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m822[0m[39m:          int64_t exponent = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint64_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mlog10[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmy_fabs[0m[1;39m([0m[39md[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m823[0m[39m:          double mantissa = d [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mpower[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, exponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m824[0m[39m:          k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m825[0m[39m:          n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m826[0m[39m:          [0m[1;35mout[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc, param[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m827[0m[39m:          n++;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m828[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m  k = [0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m829[0m[39m:          n += [0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a **stack-buffer-overflow** in the `%e` and `%E` format [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifier handling within `mg_vxprintf`. The analysis reveals two critical defects:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Insufficient Buffer Size**: Line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m of `src/fmt.c` declares `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` - [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Size Parameter Mismatch**: Line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m calls `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with size parameter `[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m`, but the actual buffer is only [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis allows `mg_dtoa` to write up to [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes into an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte buffer, causing a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack overflow detected by AddressSanitizer at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte past the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m buffer boundary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Pattern Inconsistency[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll other numeric format specifiers in the codebase follow a consistent pattern:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `%d`, `%u`, `%x`, `%X`, `%p`, `%g`, `%f`: Use `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m275[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for size parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only `%e` and `%E`: Deviate with `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and hardcoded size `[0m[1;36m10[0m[39m`[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Trigger Path[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered through:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `mg_http_parse` → detects Content-Length > [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m097[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m152[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `MG_ERROR` macro → logs error with `%e` format[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `mg_log` → calls `mg_vxprintf`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `mg_vxprintf` → processes `%e` format specifier[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Stack overflow occurs in `mg_dtoa` → `mg_snprintf` chain[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Previous Patch Analysis[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `test/tls_multirec/patched_mongoose.c` file shows a previous [0m[32m"fix"[0m[39m that [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompletely removed the `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` format specifier handling. This is an overly [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maggressive approach that breaks functionality and would cause test failures in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`test/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3654[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3662[0m[39m`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Changes Required[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: src/fmt.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m322[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m from:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m from:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: mongoose.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m824[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince `mongoose.c` is an amalgamation file containing the same code, apply [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical changes:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m from:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m824[0m[39m from:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistency with Codebase**: This fix aligns `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` handlers with the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished pattern used by all other numeric format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%g`, `%f`, `%d`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`%u`, `%x`, `%X`, `%p`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Adequate Buffer Space**: [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_dtoa` uses an internal [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/fmt.[0m[1;92mc:139[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mantissa formatting can produce ~[0m[1;36m15[0m[39m significant digits + decimal point + sign [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m≈ [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m chars[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exponent via `mg_lld` can produce up to [0m[1;36m21[0m[39m chars for int64_t [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthough typically[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmuch smaller[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes provides safe margin for both operations[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type-Safe Size Calculation**: Using `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of hardcoded [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mliterals prevents future errors if buffer size changes[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: Unlike the previous patch that removed `%e`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`%E` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupport, this fix maintains full compatibility with existing tests and expected [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: Only two lines per file need modification, reducing risk of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserved Logic[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All format specifier parsing logic remains unchanged[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Mantissa and exponent calculation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m320[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m321[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m826[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m unchanged[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Output logic via `scpy` and `out` unchanged[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Scientific notation formatting behavior unchanged[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing tests in `test/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3654[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3662[0m[39m` will continue to pass[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effect Mitigation[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Stack Memory Usage**: Increasing buffer from [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes adds [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes to the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack frame of `mg_vxprintf`. This is negligible:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function already allocates a [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer for other format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m275[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other local variables exist in the same frame[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes is insignificant for typical stack sizes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mseveral MB[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No recursion concerns as `mg_vxprintf` call depth is bounded[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Performance**: No performance impact - the buffer size change doesn't affect [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution speed, only stack allocation which happens once per format string [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
